						<!-- firstHeading -->
			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading">移动网络代码</h1>
			<!-- /firstHeading -->
			<!-- bodyContent -->
			<div id="bodyContent">
								<!-- tagline -->
				<div id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
				<!-- /tagline -->
								<!-- subtitle -->

								<!-- bodycontent -->
				<div lang="zh" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><table class="metadata plainlinks ambox ambox-content" style="">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image">
<div style="width: 52px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Translation_arrow_zh.svg" class="image" title="翻译标记"><img alt="翻译标记" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Translation_arrow_zh.svg/60px-Translation_arrow_zh.svg.png" width="60" height="18" /></a></div>
</td>
<td class="mbox-text" style=""><b>当前条目的内容正在依照其他语言维基百科的内容进行<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E7%BF%BB%E8%AF%91%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82" title="Wikipedia:翻译请求">翻译</a>。</b><small><i>（2012年1月16日）</i></small><br />
<small>如果您熟知条目内容并擅长翻译，欢迎协助<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="//zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E7%A7%BB%E5%8A%A8%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%BB%A3%E7%A0%81&amp;action=edit">改善或校对这篇条目</a></span>。长期闲置的非中文内容可能会被移除。</small></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>移动网络代码</b>（Mobile Network Code，MNC）是与<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A7%BB%E5%8A%A8%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E4%BB%A3%E7%A0%81&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="移动国家代码">移动国家代码</a>（Mobile Country Code，MCC）（也称为“MCC / MNC元组”）相结合用于唯一的表记一个移动电话的运营商。这些运营商可以是使用的<a href="/w/index.php?title=GSM/LTE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="GSM/LTE">GSM/LTE</a>、<a href="/wiki/CDMA" title="CDMA" class="mw-redirect">CDMA</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E6%88%90%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%97%E5%A2%9E%E5%BC%BA%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C" title="集成数字增强网络">iDEN</a>、<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%B0%E9%9D%A2%E9%9B%86%E7%BE%A4%E6%97%A0%E7%BA%BF%E7%94%B5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="地面集群无线电">TETRA</a>和<a href="/wiki/UMTS" title="UMTS">UMTS</a><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E9%99%86%E5%9C%B0%E7%A7%BB%E5%8A%A8%E7%BD%91&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="公众陆地移动网">公众陆地移动网</a>亦或是<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%AB%E6%98%9F" title="卫星" class="mw-redirect">卫星</a>移动网络。<a href="/wiki/ITU-T" title="ITU-T" class="mw-redirect">ITU-T</a>协议E.212中定义移动国家代码。</p>
<p><br />
下表包含完整的移动电话运营商列表。出于国家信息被提供的完整性，最好其信息引用自移动<a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_mobile_country_codes&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="List of mobile country codes">国家代码页</a>的列表，同样其中信息与<a href="/w/index.php?title=ISO_3166-1_alpha-2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ISO 3166-1 alpha-2">ISO3166-1</a>国家代码交叉引用。</p>
<p><br />
The MNC and MCC values within the table below, appear to be <a href="/w/index.php?title=Decimal&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Decimal">decimal</a> numbers, however when working with various <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mobile_phone&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Mobile phone">mobile phone</a> <a href="/wiki/SDK" title="SDK" class="mw-redirect">SDK</a>s, such as the <a href="/wiki/BlackBerry" title="BlackBerry" class="mw-redirect">BlackBerry</a> developer <a href="/wiki/SDK" title="SDK" class="mw-redirect">SDK</a>, the values returned by device APIs are encoded with <a href="/w/index.php?title=Binary-coded_decimal&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Binary-coded decimal">Binary-coded decimal</a>.</p>
<p><br /></p>

<h2><span class="editsection">[<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A7%BB%E5%8A%A8%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%BB%A3%E7%A0%81&amp;action=edit&amp;section=262" title="编辑段落：外部链接">编辑</a>]</span> <span class="mw-headline" id=".E5.A4.96.E9.83.A8.E9.93.BE.E6.8E.A5">外部链接</span></h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=International_Telecommunication_Union&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International Telecommunication Union">International Telecommunication Union</a> list of MNCs <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.itu.int/dms_pub/itu-t/opb/sp/T-SP-E.212B-2010-PDF-E.pdf">ITU.int</a></li>

<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.prepaidgsm.net/">PrePaidGSM.net - Up to date information on GSM mobile prepaid cards offered</a>, including MCC/MNC information</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.numberingplans.com/">Numberingplans.com</a>, International Numbering Plans</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.proxicast.com/support/cell-carriers.htm">3G Cellular Router manufacturer Proxicast's downloadable list of over 900 worldwide CDMA/GSM/UMTS mobile networks</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.itu.int/ITU-T/inr/forms/mnc.html">Assignment or withdrawal of Mobile Network Code (MNC) for the international identification plan for mobile users (According to ITU-T Recommendation E.212)</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.radioraiders.com/gsm-mobile-network-codes.php">Radioraiders.com</a> On-Line MNC Calculator - Converts MNC/MCC to Network Name and Country</li>
<li>Latvian <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.sprk.gov.lv/?setl=2">SPRK.gov.lv</a> Public Utilities Commission is an independent state institution responsible for regulation of energy, telecommunications, post and railway sectors in accordance with the law "On Regulators of Public Utilities" and the corresponding normative acts in the regulated sectors.</li>
<li>Tapaci</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.42it.eu/Mobile_Systems/SMS/Coverage/UK/">42it.eu</a>, Mobile Operator Codes (UK)</li>
<li>Malaysian Communications and Multimedia Commission (MCMC) Numbering Management <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.skmm.gov.my/index.php?c=public&amp;v=art_view&amp;art_id=228">[20]</a></li>
</ul>
